Daily Routines & Time-Blocking\n\nTom Ferry's ideal agent day follows the **SAVERS** framework (from Hal Elrod's \"Miracle Morning\"):\n\n**Morning Routine (6:00-8:00 AM):**\n- **Silence/Meditation**: Deep, slow breaths to calm the mind and push away distractions\n- **Affirmations**: Spoken in present tense (e.g., \"I make $250,000\" not \"I want to make...\"). Signature affirmation: \"I'm a lean, mean, appointment setting machine!\"\n- **Visualization**: Visualize the top 3 goals for the day as already achieved\n- **Exercise**: Gym, running, or stretching\n- **Reading**: Professional development\n- **Scribing/Journaling**: Write gratitude, wins achieved, and intentions for the day\n\n**Hour-by-Hour Daily Schedule:**\n- **8:00-9:00 AM** - Prep and market review\n- **9:00-10:30 AM** - Appointment setting and prospecting (NON-NEGOTIABLE)\n- **10:30-11:00 AM** - Break: recharge with a walk, check phone\n- **11:00 AM-12:00 PM** - Lunch + education (watch a TED Talk, listen to a podcast)\n- **12:00-4:30 PM** - Appointments + listing presentations (if calendar is light, jump back into prospecting)\n- **4:30-5:00 PM** - Daily wrap-up: review what worked, what didn't, track wins and lessons\n- **5:00-7:00 PM** - Home, dinner, family time\n\n**Prospecting Power Hours:** Two designated blocks daily -- 9:00-11:00 AM and 4:00-6:00 PM. Agents schedule both but only need to complete ONE of the two daily, creating an \"illusion of choice\" that boosts compliance. Four hours should be blocked on the calendar Monday-Friday for appointment setting. Agents doing more than 5 hours/week of prospecting are the ones making over $200,000/year.\n\n---\n\n### 2. Lead Generation Methods\n\nTom Ferry teaches a **diversified, multi-channel lead generation** approach. He recommends agents combine referrals, events, and local networking with digital systems like search, paid ads, and content marketing. Specific methods include:\n\n- **Expired Listings**: Scripts for handling objections like \"We didn't get the price we wanted\" or \"Interest rates are so high we figured we'd wait\"\n- **FSBOs (For Sale By Owner)**: Drive through your area, identify FSBOs, and make cold calls. Script: \"Hi, I'm [name] working for [company], I'm looking for the owner of the home for sale...\"\n- **Circle Prospecting**: Call homeowners in a radius around your open house address or recent listing\n- **Door Knocking**: Script: \"Hi, my name is [name] with [company], how are you today? I wanted to give you a quick update on the real estate market. Last month, we sold [X] homes, with [X] selling above the asking price...\"\n- **Mega Open Houses**: Large-scale events with sign-in sheets capturing name, phone, email, permission to follow up, and qualifying questions. Set a stretch goal for appointments within 30 days. Goal Setting Framework\n\nTom Ferry uses a **reverse-engineering** methodology:\n\n1. Start with your annual **GCI (Gross Commission Income)** goal\n2. Convert to required **units** (transactions) based on average commission\n3. Plug in your **conversion rates** (listing appointments to signed listings, buyer consultations to signed agreements, signed to closed)\n4. Calculate required **appointments per year**, then per week\n5. Back into **daily talk-to numbers** based on your conversations-per-appointment ratio\n\nFormula: GCI Goal → Units → Conversion Rates → Appointments/Year → Appointments/Week → Daily Conversations\n\nUses a **SMART Goals template** and business plan worksheet. Mindset & Accountability\n\n**Mindset Philosophy:**\n- \"You're either fueling your future with your mindset or you are staying parked in the past\"\n- Mindset is the MOST important thing clients must focus on, per Buffini coaches\n- \"You are what you think and believe\"\n- Gratitude is central: \"No matter what the circumstances are, a sense of gratitude is what it's all about\"\n- Faith-based undertones: Brian Buffini's Irish Catholic background influences his approach, with emphasis on spiritual life, purpose, and values\n- \"It's a Good Life\" podcast: 10 million+ downloads covering personal growth, gratitude, habits, and faith\n\n**Accountability Structure:**\n- **One2One Coaching**: 2 coaching sessions per month with a Certified Business Coach\n- Coaches are **full-time professionals** trained in Buffini's system (not part-time agents)\n- Coaches have collaboratively served with 1.7 million coaching calls and more than 1 million hours of coaching\n- Coach helps define goals, develop a business plan, track progress, and adjust plans\n- Peer accountability groups among coaching members between individual coaching calls\n- Accountability partner is described as \"the secret ingredient to achieving your goals\"\n\n---\n\n### 6. Marketing Strategies\n\nBuffini's marketing is **relationship-focused, not mass-market**:\n\n- **Monthly Referral Maker PRO Marketing Kit** (delivered to your door):\n  - Print mailers + cover letters that educate and inspire\n  - Coordinating notecards for handwritten messages\n  - Stickers and additional materials\n  - Digital eReports (infographics on home improvement, personal growth -- content clients actually want)\n  - Pop-by tag library\n  - Schedule telling you when to send each piece\n- **Personal Handwritten Notes**: Emphasized as the key differentiator. A handwritten note shows clients you care and sets you apart\n- **Client Appreciation Parties**: BBQs, bowling parties, ice cream socials, wine tastings, holiday events. Budget as part of annual business plan. One member's $1,200 event generated 4 referrals in 2 weeks\n- **Pop-Bys**: Small seasonal gifts delivered in person with referral reminder tags\n- **Email Marketing**: eReports and digital content shared via email\n- Buffini does NOT heavily emphasize social media, video marketing, or paid digital advertising the way Tom Ferry does\n\n---\n\n### 7. Client Relationship & Referral Systems\n\nThis is Buffini's **core competency** and primary differentiator:\n\n- **Database Classification (A+ through D)**:\n  - **A+**: Have sent multiple referrals and would do so again -- highest touch frequency\n  - **A**: Strong relationship, have referred or would refer\n  - **B**: Good relationship, moderate contact\n  - **C**: Cool acquaintances -- less frequent contact\n  - **D**: Dead to you -- delete from database\n- **Systematic Touch Plan**: Calls + notes + pop-bys + monthly mailers + eReports + client parties\n- **Pop-By Strategy**: The \"quickest and most effective way to generate referrals.\" Deliver a small gift, briefly \"pop by\" the client's home, leave it on doorstep if not home. Tags remind clients you're never too busy for referrals\n- **Client Parties**: Annual/quarterly events for A+ clients. Themes: summer BBQ, holiday events, \"Reverse Pop-Bys\" (clients come to you to pick up items like holiday baskets)\n- **Notes to Local Businesses**: Show appreciation for their business and referrals, extending the referral network beyond past clients\n- **\"Working by Referral\" Philosophy**: Rather than targeting strangers, focus marketing on people you already have relationships with\n\n---\n\n### 8. Transaction Management\n\n- **Pathway to Mastery -- Essentials** (8 weeks): Working by Referral fundamentals, working with buyers and sellers, negotiation, business planning\n- **Pathway to Mastery -- Advanced**: Deep dive into objection handling, pricing presentations, showings, the entire buying and selling process start to finish\n- **100 Days to Greatness**: 14-week program for newer agents covering everything needed to launch a career, generating an average of $75,500 and 7 transactions during the course\n- **Referral Maker CRM**: Tracks client relationships through the transaction pipeline\n- Buffini does not publish detailed transaction checklists/SOPs the way Tom Ferry does; the focus is more on relationship management than operational process documentation\n\n---\n\n### 9. Goal Setting Framework\n\nBuffini uses the **\"Five Circles of Life\"** framework:\n\n1. **Spiritual**: Faith, purpose, values\n2. **Family**: Relationships, marriage, children\n3. **Business**: Career growth, production\n4. **Financial**: Income, savings, investments, debt reduction\n5. **Personal**: Health, hobbies, self-care, personal development\n\n**Goal Timeframes:**\n- **10-Day Goals** (short-range): Achievable in 2 weeks; create momentum\n- **3-Month / 10-Month Goals** (mid-range): Achievable within the year\n- **5-Year Goals** (long-range): Vision and life planning\n\n**Reverse-Engineering:**\n- Enter income goal into Referral Maker CRM along with tax rate, splits, commission amount, business expenses, and current sales volume\n- System calculates transactions needed and generates daily/weekly/monthly activity goals\n- Break ambitious goals into smaller goals within specific timeframes\n\n**\"5 Circle Fit\"**: When all five circles are in healthy balance. The concept emphasizes that devoting yourself only to business leads to burnout, stress, and poor relationships.\n\n---\n\n### 10. Key Differentiators\n\n- **Largest real estate coaching and training company in North America** with 30 years of experience\n- **Pure referral-based system**: No cold calling, no door knocking, no chasing strangers. The entire philosophy centers on nurturing existing relationships\n- **Full-time professional coaches** (not part-time agents) -- certified through rigorous training with ongoing weekly skill-building\n- **Integrated done-for-you marketing**: Monthly kits with mailers, notecards, pop-by tags, and digital content delivered to your door\n- **Holistic life approach**: The Five Circles framework addresses spiritual, family, financial, and personal life alongside business -- not just production numbers\n- **Brian Buffini's personal story**: Irish immigrant who built a real estate empire through relationships. His authenticity and personal brand are central\n- **\"It's a Good Life\" podcast**: 10 million+ downloads; one of the most popular real estate/personal development podcasts\n- **Referral Maker CRM**: Purpose-built for the referral system with A+ through D classification\n- **The Blitz**: Three annual lead-gen sprints that generate concentrated results\n- **Best suited for**: Agents who already have a sphere of influence and prefer relationship-building over aggressive prospecting\n- **Potential weakness**: May be less effective for brand-new agents in a new area without an established network; some agents find the approach \"too soft\"\n\n---\n\n### 11. Recommended Weekly Schedule\n\nBuffini does NOT publish a rigid sample weekly schedule like Tom Ferry. Instead, the system generates a **personalized daily activity plan** based on:\n- Your income goal\n- Your database size and quality\n- Your client rankings (A+ through D)\n- The algorithm's comparison with other successful Buffini agents at similar income levels\n\n**Core weekly activities include:**\n- Daily calls to database contacts (number determined by CRM algorithm)\n- Daily handwritten personal notes\n- Weekly pop-by visits to A+ and A clients\n- Monthly marketing mailer distribution\n- Mid-month eReport email sends\n- Quarterly client appreciation events\n- Three Blitz lead-generation sprints per year (approximately 60 days each)\n\n---\n\n### 12. Success Metrics / KPIs Tracked\n\n- **Daily activities completed**: Calls made, notes written, pop-bys delivered\n- **Referrals received** (the primary leading indicator in Buffini's system)\n- **Transactions closed**\n- **Income earned vs. income goal**\n- **Database size and quality** (A+ through D distribution)\n- **Contact frequency compliance** (are you hitting your scheduled touches?)\n- **Blitz results**: Additional transactions and income generated during sprint periods\n- **Win the Day completion**: Daily activity scorecard\n- **10-day, 3-month, and annual goal progress**\n\nThe Referral Maker CRM tracks these metrics and creates a personal \"scoreboard\" to celebrate small wins and stay accountable.\n\n---\n\n---\n\n## HEAD-TO-HEAD COMPARISON SUMMARY\n\n| Dimension | Tom Ferry | Buffini & Company |\n|-----------|-----------|-------------------|\n| **Core Philosophy** | Diversified, aggressive prospecting + digital marketing | Relationship-based, referral-only system |\n| **Lead Gen Approach** | Cold calling, expired listings, FSBOs, door knocking, circle prospecting, online ads, open houses, SOI | Calls, notes, pop-bys to existing database; no cold prospecting |\n| **Daily Structure** | Rigid hour-by-hour schedule with non-negotiable prospecting blocks | Personalized CRM-generated daily activity plan |\n| **Scripts** | Extensive public script library; memorization + roleplay emphasis | Proprietary \"dialogues\"; conversational, relational tone |\n| **Mindset** | SAVERS morning routine, affirmations, visualization, journaling | Five Circles of Life, gratitude, faith, holistic balance |\n| **Accountability** | 2-48 sessions/year depending on tier; part-time agent-coaches | 2 sessions/month; full-time professional coaches |\n| **Marketing** | Video-first, social media, digital ads, direct mail farming | Done-for-you monthly marketing kits, handwritten notes, pop-bys |\n| **Technology** | Follow Up Boss, Ylopo, The Hub, heavy tech stack | Referral Maker CRM (purpose-built for referral system) |\n| **Events** | Success Summit (7,000+ agents), high energy | MasterMind Summit (personal growth focus), intimate |\n| **Best For** | Agents wanting aggressive growth, digital marketing, diverse lead sources | Agents with existing SOI who prefer relationship nurturing |\n| **Coaching Style** | High-energy, push-oriented, metrics-driven | Relational, supportive, life-balance focused |\n| **Pricing** | $6,000-$12,000+/year | Varies by tier; generally more accessible entry points |\n\n---\n\nSources:\n-
